The Liaoning Case is Postponed for Resolution; League of Nations and China and Japan Issue Declarations

=China= The Draft is Evasive and Disappointing

=Japan= Repeatedly Insists on Protecting Vested Rights

=League of Nations= Mediation is Difficult, but Sincerity is Not Completely Exhausted

(Geneva) The Information Office of the Chinese Delegation issued a notice explaining that the Chinese government believes that the first draft resolution of the Committee of Nineteen is disappointing for the following reasons: ㈠ The resolution did not declare opposition to "Manchukuo" nor did it state that Japan violated the League of Nations Covenant and other international treaties. ㈡ The resolution did not include arbitration methods, nor did it include the important explanations of the Lytton Report. ㈢ Although the resolution mentions Chapter Ten of the Lytton Report, it is completely inappropriate and will inevitably encounter fierce resistance from the Chinese people. ㈣ The resolution does not specify the dates requested by China. (20th Havas Dispatch)

(Geneva) The Japanese Delegation issued a statement to the press tonight, expressing its admiration for the Committee of Nineteen's resolution to seek a constructive solution to the Sino-Japanese dispute. It also stated that the Japanese Delegation believes that its duty lies in sincerely striving to ensure that the work undertaken in Geneva achieves a successful conclusion in a way that both protects Japan's rights and affirms peace in the Far East and consolidates the League of Nations' cause. (20th Reuters Dispatch)

(Geneva) The Chairman of the Committee of Nineteen, Foreign Minister Hymans of Belgium, was absent and was replaced by Swiss representative Huber. He recently issued the following statement: First, the Sino-Japanese problem involves substantive difficulties on the one hand, and takes a considerable amount of time due to the exchange of telegrams on the other, so its negotiations will take a considerable amount of time. This is unavoidable. The Sino-Japanese dispute has been going on for a long time, and one of the parties has requested that the date to which the covenant stipulates be extended be specified. The Committee is deeply aware of the need to resolve this matter quickly, but because this matter is of great importance, the various issues it raises involve the entirety of the issue of world cooperation, and the new system of international relations is currently in progress and is also affected by these issues. Therefore, the Committee must deal with it with extreme perseverance and cannot rush to a conclusion before exhausting its mediation efforts. The resolution drafted by the Committee is generally acceptable to both parties. Although there are currently wide differences of opinion, they are not irreconcilable if dealt with sincerely. In order to avoid failure and the impact of failure, mediation and negotiation are necessary measures. Therefore, the Committee of Nineteen has decided to allow the necessary time to conduct talks with the countries concerned and to allow the governments of all countries to participate in order to seek a solution. The next meeting will be held no later than January 16. The Committee believes that both parties will be able to show concessions during this period. Otherwise, mediation will be impossible. (20th Havas Dispatch)

Ambassadors Gu and Guo Return to Their Original Posts

Su Bingwen's Former Troops in Russia are Suffering Due to Lack of Supplies

Karakhan Requests that Our Government Provide Assistance

Su Himself Remains in Moscow

(Moscow) The Soviet government bulletin "Izvestia" stated that Soviet Deputy Foreign Minister Karakhan recently met with Chinese representative Wang Zengsi to discuss ways to deal with the troops of Su Bingwen's former subordinates who remained in Russian territory. Karakhan told Representative Wang that there were 2,890 soldiers of Su's troops who had entered Russian territory, and 1,200 civilians, including 347 women and 206 children. The Soviet government has allowed them to leave the country, but they are trapped by economic difficulties, having neither the travel expenses to return home nor the means to live. The Soviet government feels that it cannot bear the travel expenses or long-term supplies for these people, so it hopes that China will provide the necessary assistance. Before this method is resolved, they will temporarily remain in Tomsk. Representative Wang promised to report this to the Chinese government immediately. (20th TASS Dispatch)

(Moscow) When Su Bingwen's troops retreated last month, a total of 4,090 Chinese soldiers and civilians retreated into Russian territory, including 1,200 civilians, of whom 347 were women and 306 were children. According to Russian newspapers, Russian Deputy Foreign Minister Karakhan has today discussed the method of dealing with the situation with Secretary-General Wang of the Sino-Russian Conference. Karakhan believes that these people are poor and that the Russian government cannot sell them out of the country or maintain their supplies for free. He hopes that the Chinese government will quickly find a way to transport them back to their country. For the time being, these people will be left in the territory of Tomsk. Secretary-General Wang promised to report to the government immediately. (20th Reuters Dispatch)

(Beijing) Su Bingwen's secretary-general, He Shengda, telegraphed from Beijing on the 18th, stating that after Su and others arrived in Moscow, they met with Shi Lin and other important figures. They plan to stay in Moscow for one week to travel and give lectures in various cities. They will not leave Russia until Mo Dehui returns to Moscow. All newspapers have written extremely respectful editorials on Su. A welcome party was held in Moscow on the 17th, with 20,000 people participating. (21st Dispatch)

(Beijing) Su Bingwen's son, Zongjun, said that in this recent general offensive by the Japanese army in northern Manchuria, the great battle lasted seven days and nights. The casualties of the National Salvation Army reached four to five thousand people. The battle was fierce, no less than the Shanghai Battle. The area is remote, traffic is obstructed, and news is not timely. For more than two months from September 27, there was very little domestic assistance. After his father returns to China and negotiates a proper agreement, he will definitely reorganize his forces and continue to resist Japan. (21st Dispatch)

Chen Jitang Telegraphes Yan, Gu, and Guo

Hoping to Strive According to the Covenant

If the Japanese Side is Unreasonably Tyrannical

There is Only a National Mobilization

(Guangzhou) Chen Jitang telegraphed Luo [Wen'gan], Minister of Foreign Affairs, and forwarded to Envoys Yan [Huiqing], Gu [Weijun], and Guo [Taiqi] on the 21st: "Japan took advantage of our unpreparedness, occupied our Northeast with violence, and forcibly kidnapped the deposed emperor Puyi to organize a puppet government, attempting to repeat the old tricks of annexing Korea and destroying our country. The facts of its displaying of power without revealing justice, its disregard for the League of Nations, and its destruction of world peace are obvious. People around the world do not know this. Recently, with exhausted arguments, it used despicable means at the League of Nations General Assembly to falsely accuse our country of being an disunified nation, hoping to shift the world's attention and cover up its crimes. Its intentions are sinister and hateful. In addition to telegraphing the Central Government to actively prepare for war, we are also actively preparing for mobilization at any time. I hope that you will negotiate and preside over the discussions, uphold justice based on the League of Nations Covenant, and not stop until the goal of recovering lost territory is achieved. If they are unreasonably tyrannical, then we can only mobilize the whole country to fight to the death. Although the ox is thin, it is still angry with the pig. We are not afraid of death. The telegram is full of grief and indignation. I cannot express it all." (21st Dispatch)

The Cemetery for Martyrs Who Died Resisting Japan Adopts a Representative System for Burial

128 People Selected

(Nanjing) The Cemetery Committee for Martyrs Who Died Resisting Japan has located the address of the cemetery at the foot of Zijin Mountain, east of Linggu Temple and west of Tan's Tomb, in front of the Memorial Hall. Because the address is narrow, it was decided to adopt a representative system for burial, using a lottery method. After the lottery, 70 people from the 19th Route Army, 58 people from the 5th Army, the Gendarmerie, the Volunteer Army, etc., a total of 128 people, were selected, as a commemoration of the eternally remembered January 28th Shanghai Incident. Officials have already gone to Wuxi, Kunshan, Taicang, Shanghai, Wusong, and other places with the adjutants of the concerned armies to search for the remains. After they are found, they will be transported to Nanjing and buried on a selected date. (21st Dispatch)

He Zhi Chong Telegraphes Requesting Prompt Dispatch of He Jiwu to Guizhou

To Concurrently Serve as Chairman

(Nanjing) He Zhi Chong, Commander of Bandit Suppression in the Hunan-Guizhou Border Region, telegraphed Chairman Lin, Chairman Jiang, President Song, and Minister He, stating that the upheavals in Guizhou stemmed from military and civilian rule, with those with military status vying for power. Since the reform of Guizhou's provincial administration, political crises have occurred frequently. Now, the 25th Army is continuing the tradition of military rule, resulting in infighting and internal strife. Now that Chairman Wang has left the province due to certain matters, and all the department heads have closed their doors, the political center is suspended and masterless. The people of Guizhou are extremely anxious. I earnestly request that He Jiwu be promptly dispatched to take office and concurrently serve as Chairman, so that Guizhou's administration is not interrupted and disputes are prevented. If Committee Member He travels to Guizhou from Hunan, I, Zhi Chong, will do my best to protect him and support the implementation of the Central Government's orders to the end. Whether this is appropriate is up to your discretion. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) After Mao Guangxiang occupied Guiyang, he telegraphed the Central Government one after another, expressing his extreme support. He asked the Central Government to command him to take full responsibility for settling the Guizhou situation. The telegram did not explicitly order him to preside over the Guizhou administration. Japanese Troops on Jinzhou-Chaoyang Line Shelling Daily

Planes Dropping Bombs ‖ Machine Gun Strafing

Tang Yulin Orders Dong's Brigade to Strictly Guard the Borders of Rehe

The Volunteer Army Adopts a Strategy of Decentralization and Guerrilla Warfare

Jinzhou is Overwhelmed with Rumors

(Beijing) Armored trains of the Japanese army stationed on the Jinzhou-Chaoyang Line have been shelling villages near the railway in the Nanling area for several days. At the same time, they are dropping bombs from planes and strafing with machine guns. Tang Yulin has ordered Dong's Brigade to strictly guard Yanshan, Nanchangpenggou, and other places on the border of Rehe. The traitor Li Zirong received 5,000 yuan in border industry notes from the Japanese army headquarters in Jin County and held a meeting with the leaders of the Dongwen Society in that area, planning to form a militia. Li recently went to Shenyang to discuss specific implementation methods with the Japanese army headquarters. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry, in view of the economic decline in rural areas and the urgent need for relief, has issued a general order to all provinces, ordering local areas to cooperate with merchants to establish rural credit cooperatives to circulate rural finance. Ordinary banks and money shops in various places mostly focus on short-term loans, which are difficult to suit farmers' loans. A New Fascist Party Appears in Japan, Named the National League, with Adachi and Nakano as Leaders, Advocating East Asian Monroe Doctrine and Economic Merger of Japan and Manchuria

▲Reuters, Tokyo, 21st - The trend of hostility towards existing political parties in Japan is growing daily. In recent months, political groups resembling "棒喝" (a Zen term implying sudden awakening) have sprung up one after another. The most important of these is the group initiated by the former Minister of Home Affairs, Adachi. Adachi left the Minseito Party and established the National Policy Research Society, with Nakano, who possesses leadership abilities, as his assistant. With the goal of upholding the existing parliamentary system but eliminating the existing bad habits of political parties, it has gained many supporters since its establishment. It has been decided to hold the founding ceremony of the new political party tomorrow, with 8,000 representatives from various places participating. The new political party will be named the National League. Its political platform includes the Far Eastern Monroe Doctrine and the economic merger of Japan and Manchuria. It also advocates major reforms in matters such as taxes, finance, education, and diplomacy. At the time of the new party's establishment, its strength in the Diet has already reached 33 votes, and the populist Diet member Matsutani has officially switched allegiance to the new party today. The National League is an organization of a Fascist nature, so members plan to use black shirts as part of their uniforms. Today, Nakano told reporters that this party especially welcomes young people from all over the country. He estimates that no less than two million people support this party and expects the number of members to increase rapidly after its official establishment.

Class Struggle in Japan Intensifies

More than 6,000 Communists Arrested

1,500 Convicted

▲Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 21st - According to investigations by our agency's correspondent, since the Tanaka Cabinet, the Japanese government has arrested more than 6,000 suspected Communists. More than 2,000 people were arrested in the March 15th Incident alone, of whom 511 were convicted. The number of people arrested and reported in the April 16th Incident and in between exceeded 1,500, with 400 convicted. In 1930, more than 1,500 people were arrested, with 460 convicted. From 1931 to mid-September of this year, another 1,500 people were arrested, of whom 1,115 were from the three prefectures of Osaka, Hyogo, and Kyoto, with 185 convicted. The above figures total more than 6,000 people. Other communist incidents in Taiwan, Korea, and other colonies are not included. Currently, the number of convicted prisoners in jail has reached 1,557, while others are still being questioned. The intensification of internal class struggle in the warrior state can be seen from this.

US President Approves Philippine Import Tariffs

Chinese Goods Exported to the Philippines Greatly Affected

▲National News Agency, Washington, 20th - The White House notified the Department of the Army today that the new tariff bill passed by the Philippine Legislative Assembly has been signed by the President and will take effect immediately. The bill contains many provisions to prevent the dumping of foreign goods. The tariff rates are as high as 100% of the value, and the price of gold bars in the currency of the country of origin is used as the standard for taxation. In addition, it specifically increases the import tax on meat, eggs, and cured meat. Therefore, China's trade with the Philippines will be greatly affected.

Roosevelt's Attitude Towards War Debts

Does Not Approve of Combining it with Disarmament

Refuses to Recommend Committee Members to Join the Consideration

▲Reuters, New York, 21st - Today's New York Times stated that Roosevelt is unwilling to take any action to hinder immediate action on the war debt issue, but in a reply to President Hoover, he does not agree with the plan to organize a committee to consider the matter and does not want to recommend committee members. Roosevelt believes that the existing institutions are sufficient to re-examine the debt-paying ability of debtor countries, and there is no need to organize a separate organization. Roosevelt also does not approve of combining the war debt issue with the World Economic Conference and disarmament issues. Roosevelt believes that war debts are a separate issue. The New York Times also stated that Roosevelt plans to issue an order after taking office as president on March 4, instructing Owen Young, known for the Young Plan, and economic expert Bernard Baruch to re-engage in the study of the war debt issue.

Schleicher Implements Moderate Policies After Taking Office

Promulgates New Order Maintaining Domestic Order

Lifts Ban on the Return of the Former Emperor

▲Reuters, Berlin, 3rd - German Chancellor Schleicher is now striving to create a more moderate situation throughout the country. He has taken his first step today, issuing a presidential emergency decree aimed at maintaining domestic peace. Signed by the President, the Chancellor, and the Minister of the Interior, it rescinds various emergency decrees promulgated during the von Papen era, such as the establishment of special courts to severely punish political prisoners and the forced publication of government announcements in newspapers. However, various provisions in the Law for the Protection of the Republic, such as the disciplinary articles on acts that insult the president, the government, the country, the national flag, the navy, and the army, will be retained. As for the ban on the return of the German former emperor, it has now been lifted. Since this article has not been effective in the past two years, the former emperor can now return to the country freely in a private capacity.

Lewd Customs in the Japanese Archipelago

Statistics Released by the Japanese Ministry of Home Affairs

210,000 Registered Prostitutes

Over 22 Million Customers

Secret Prostitution Not Included

▲Hualian News Agency - According to a survey by the Japanese Ministry of Home Affairs, in 1931, the total number of prostitutes nationwide (in the Japanese mainland) was 210,681, and the number of customers was 22,239,641. The detailed contents are as follows: (1931 Statistics from the Ministry of Home Affairs) Geishas: 77,280; Hostesses: 81,301; Prostitutes: 52,100; Total: 210,681. According to the above figures, each prostitute entertains an average of 106 customers per year. However, these figures only refer to registered prostitutes. The number of secret prostitutes is not included. In light of the actual situation in Japan, secret prostitution usually exceeds public prostitution by more than two times. Therefore, the number of Japanese women who make a living by relying on their bodies is more than 600,000, and the number of customers is as high as 60 million.

Government Hires German Engineers to Dredge the Yellow River

Technical Experiments Conducted on the Shores of Lake Walchensee

▲Havas, Berlin, 21st - The evening newspaper reports that the waters of the Yellow River in China have historically caused disasters due to frequent flooding. The Chinese government has now decided to entrust the responsibility of dredging the Yellow River to German engineers. The Sengcheng Institute for Hydraulic Research has recently conducted technical experiments near Lake Walchensee in the Bavarian Alps for this matter. The method involves excavating a waterway to simulate the flow of the Yellow River, and placing cohesive sandy soil in the waterway, with a composition roughly equivalent to the alluvial soil contained in the Yellow River, to study the expansion and contraction of alluvial soil in the Yellow River. After the results of this experiment are obtained, a committee consisting of several engineers will be sent to China to conduct on-site surveys.

Large Fire in Niigata Prefecture, Japan, More Than 500 Households Reduced to Ashes

▲Den-tsu, Takada, 21st - This morning, a fire suddenly broke out in the tenements of the Yamagishi Silk Mill in Itoigawa Town, Niigata Prefecture. The fire was extremely fierce and immediately spread to more than 500 households. It was extinguished at 9:30 a.m. Buildings such as the parking lot, tax office, post office, and employment exchange were all burned down, resulting in huge losses. There appear to be no deaths or injuries.

Northeast Problem and the League of Nations

(6)

While Chinese public opinion generally hopes that certain political privileges will be returned to China to match the dignity of Chinese national sovereignty, any intelligent Chinese person would never advocate for methods other than the internationally recognized methods of negotiation and agreement to achieve their goals. Sometimes, one might see a slogan or two on street corners, or hear a speech or two in school auditoriums, criticizing the existing basis of Sino-foreign relations. However, such slogans and speeches cannot represent the cautious attitude of the entire nation, just as the communist newspapers of Western countries do not represent the general opinion of those countries. Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the late Premier of the Chinese Kuomintang, advocated nationalism as one of the Three Principles of the People. Its nature is entirely self-defensive, peaceful, and constructive. This nationalism is the result of China's experience after interacting with various countries in the world and represents a kind of national aspiration to seek China's liberation from unequal treaties in order to achieve an equal position with other countries in the world. Therefore, its nature is purely self-defensive and peaceful. At the same time, this nationalism is also constructive. Why? Because its ultimate goal is to achieve a world commonwealth through the path of nationalism. China hopes to gradually progress and become a strong and prosperous country, so that it can contribute to world peace and happiness. It deeply understands that the final step in the progress of all countries in the world will eventually become a "nation-state," joining together in a state of great harmony. This highest political view has often been found in the words of ancient Chinese sages, Confucius being one of them. Dr. Sun Yat-sen further developed and expanded on its meaning, making it a major point in the Kuomintang's doctrine and policy. However, the Chinese people unanimously oppose Japan's traditional policy of controlling and overcoming China. With each conflict in Sino-Japanese relations, Japan's traditional policy becomes clearer, and its ability to endanger China's security and survival becomes more and more certain. The Chinese people view the current incident in the three northeastern provinces not as a local event, but as one aspect of Japan's entire continental policy. Well said are the words in the report on page 23:

"In recent years, Japan's demands have been regarded in China as a serious provocation to China's national aspirations, even more so than all the rights claimed by the powers."

The Chinese people's concept is not out of fear, but out of experience and knowledge gained over the past decades. As for other countries, China has absolutely no xenophobic intentions. From the government down to the people, all sincerely hope for the consolidation of friendly relations between China and foreign countries for mutual benefit. Regarding this point, there is no need for me to say more. Now I will only cite some figures as proof. Currently, there are 360,000 foreigners working and living peacefully in China. There are 8,200 foreign firms. Among the foreigners, there are 7,567 missionaries preaching in various parts of China without difficulty or danger. Occasional incidents are exceptions. Even many Japanese residents in China, even during this period of tense Sino-Japanese sentiment, are still able to live and work in peace under the protection of the Chinese government, with very few unexpected incidents occurring. One more thing can prove this: many Chinese state-owned enterprises employ a large number of foreign personnel. In the various ministries of the central government, there are more than 40 experts from eight countries assisting in all administrative matters, and the number is expected to increase further. The report also mentioned this point, saying:

"The National Government has recently sought and accepted international assistance in solving various problems in China, such as financial matters since 1930, and the liaison with League of Nations specialized agencies to handle economic planning and development since the establishment of the National Economic Committee in 1931, as well as flood relief work in the same year, etc."

Recently, the National Government invited the League of Nations to mediate and hired many experts to come to China to study issues such as education, hygiene, river dredging, agriculture, and sericulture. If China had any hostility towards foreign countries, such cooperation projects would not have been so successful. The criticisms made by the Japanese side against China are obviously aimed at confusing public opinion and concealing the real problem. I have already pointed out the impropriety of all its more important points. The real threat to peace in the Far East is Japan's continental policy, as mentioned above. So, what are the most important facts regarding this case that have been clarified in the report? Let me tell you. Japan has put forward many exaggerated demands in its explanation of the September 18th Incident and its subsequent actions. The Chinese government is very interested in revealing the details of the investigation report. Japan claimed that there were as many as 300 outstanding issues between China and Japan and that Japan took military action in order to resolve these outstanding issues satisfactorily. However, the report on page 66 of the investigation team states:

"However, the so-called 300 pending cases between the two countries, and the exhaustion of peaceful means by one party to resolve these cases, have not been substantiated."

The report also stated, "Therefore, the saying that all outstanding issues should be resolved by force when necessary has become a common slogan." It also stated, "All decisions to resolve by force, meetings of the General Staff Headquarters of the Army Ministry to discuss military plans, and the definite instructions issued to Commander of the Kwantung Army and Colonel Doihara, who was stationed in Fengtian and summoned to Tokyo in early September to advocate resolving all outstanding issues by force as soon as possible, were freely cited in various newspapers. Reading the records of feelings about these aspects and other organizations in various newspapers, one can know that the situation is becoming dangerously tense." Page 66 of the report also pointed out the Japanese Minister of the Army's fierce speech in Tokyo, advocating that the Japanese army in Manchuria take direct action, and pointed out the provocative acts of night exercises and occasional fire by the Japanese army in Shenyang. Finally, it mentioned the September 18th Incident, which, according to the report, was "the first step in the military occupation of Manchuria." From this, it can be seen that the fuse of the current Sino-Japanese dispute is not the unresolved outstanding issues between one country and another, but the interventionist acts of the Japanese military authorities. Also, regarding Sino-Japanese outstanding issues, the investigation team has already stated in its report that its nature can be resolved by arbitration or legal methods. Therefore, was Japan's military action on September 18th and 19th, 1931, really a self-defense action as Japan claimed? The answer to this question is of the utmost importance not only to China but also to the League of Nations, because this point is closely related to the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant. Japan claimed that the Japanese army's invasion of Manchuria was a self-defense action, but the investigation team disagreed with Japan's statement, saying:

"It is undeniable that the emotions between the Chinese and Japanese armies were high. This investigation team has obtained evidence that the Japanese side had indeed made full preparations in advance to deal with any possible war between China. This plan was put into practice on the night of September 18th to 19th, quickly and accurately. The Chinese side obeyed the instructions of their superiors (see page 69). They were neither prepared to attack the Japanese army, nor did they have a plan to harm the lives and property of the Japanese at that time or in that place. They did not concentrate on fighting against the Japanese army, nor were they ordered to fire. Therefore, they were surprised by the Japanese army's attack and its subsequent actions."

The Japanese side claimed that at about 10 p.m. on the evening of September 18th, the Chinese army blew up the South Manchurian Railway tracks near Shenyang. The Japanese side fabricated this excuse in order to use it as a fuse for its military plans. The report said, (to be continued)

The Process of Instigating Mongol Bandits to Rebel

Four Poisonous and Vicious Documents

Colonel Matsui Shot Dead: Since the September 18th and January 28th Incidents, the Japanese warlords' traditional policy of swallowing China has been actively exposed. I still remember that in March of this year, there was a so-called Mongol bandit rebellion. At that time, 5,000 Mongolian Independent Army soldiers harassed places such as Tongliao and Xining Kailu. Inner Mongolia's Declaration of Autonomy: Among the conspiratorial documents discovered at that time, there was an Inner Mongolia Declaration of Autonomy. The original text is recorded as follows: "Mongolia is a basic nation in Asia. Its origin dates back to prehistoric times. For generations, it has been independent and dominant in Asia. Until the rise of the Yuan Dynasty, it unified Europe and Asia, connecting Eastern and Western cultures, promoting material civilization, and building an unprecedented great cause. The biggest reasons why Inner Mongolia has come to this are two: the trampling of the Manchus and

The devastation of China. When the Manchus unified China, they divided Inner Mongolia into several leagues and banners, turning the entire political economy into a piecemeal political economy. The entire Inner Mongolia was divided into scattered Inner Mongolia, destroying the unified situation and replacing it with multi-headed politics. They added to its name but emptied its power, sealed its titles but seized its rights. The trick of fooling and the sinister tactics turned the innocent Inner Mongolia into a numb and indifferent one. Since the Republic of China, it has intensified, implementing a strategy of extermination in the beautiful name of republic, using the high-sounding tone of five ethnic groups as compatriots, and using the policy of assimilation. The magpie occupies the dove's nest, and the guest overpowers the host. The league and banner signboards have been changed to provinces and counties, and sacred temples have mostly become military camps. Reclamation and immigration, extortion and extortion, nothing is spared. The suffering of our Mongolian people today is even worse than that of black slaves and red races, and even worse than cattle and horses. If this continues, what can we imagine? This is why the martyrs of Inner Mongolia have risen one after another, one after another, and fought to this day. This army inherits the hot blood of the martyrs and righteous men, remembers the suffering of the nation, reverses the tide, supports the building that is about to collapse, and recovers the lost political power. The purpose is to completely realize the autonomy of Inner Mongolia. This will not only win the approval of the good compatriots of China, but also be praised and understood by the sages and wise men of all countries. Moreover, modern human beings are becoming more and more civilized, and freedom is increasing day by day. No matter what country, they are all carrying out autonomy and self-determination, enjoying the happiness that human beings should have. However, Inner Mongolia is dark and without sunshine, and it is suffering from inhuman devastation. It is not only incompatible with humanity, but also hinders evolution. This is why the people of Inner Mongolia have risen up to fight, to overthrow the magic law of mankind, and to advocate the spirit of world autonomy and self-determination. Therefore, the responsibility of this army is the responsibility of liberating the Mongolian nation, and it is also the success of the part of human coexistence and co-prosperity. I deeply hope that the young and old of the Inner Mongolian nation will rise up together, follow this army, and work together to fulfill their responsibilities. Sages and wise men of all countries who advocate humanity should jointly support it.

The Constitution of the Great Source Country: The second of the conspiratorial documents is the "Temporary Constitution for the Construction of the Great Source Republic." Its text is as follows: 1. Inner Mongolia wants to seek peace, so there is the formulation of a temporary security agreement. All banners must cooperate and abide by it. 2. Inspection Record of Suppressing Communists and Recovering Various Areas

(4)

The Situation Around Jianli

Jianli is the hometown of Wu Zixu. It faces the Yangtze River to the south, connects to Qianjiang to the north, borders Jiangling to the west, and is adjacent to the communist den of Honghu to the east. The southeast, northwest, and various regions of the county have all been communist-ized. The city was also once captured in September of the 19th year, and although it was recovered in a few months, it had been greatly damaged and recovery was not easy. Xinguizui, which belongs to it, was once the location of the Soviet of the pseudo-Hunan-Hubei-West Province of the communists, and Zhuhe was equipped with the Jianli County Soviet. The importance of its position is evident. The county was extremely brutally trampled by bandits, and one-third of the county's population was killed, especially in areas such as Fenyan and Chenhuang. As for the destruction of commercial markets and rural villages, it is even more unspeakable. Zhuhe and Xingu are both extremely large towns. After the bandit rebellion, the streets of Zhuhe were almost completely burned down, and only a few small stalls remain in Xingu today. The prosperous scene of the past can no longer be seen. The county has a total of more than 970,000 mu of farmland. After the bandit disaster and flood disaster, there are less than 920,000. Farmers have died, been injured, and fled, and the number cannot be counted. Fortunately, those who have managed to survive have no ability to cultivate, so only three-tenths of the remaining more than 900,000 mu of farmland have been cultivated, and seven-tenths of the barren land have been occupied. Farmers lack food, some use grass roots and bark to fill their hunger, and some eat water chestnuts and horse chestnuts. They are starving and freezing, and they are extremely distressed. Those who fled outside have gradually returned after the bandit area was recovered, but because of the lack of food, they cannot survive, and recently they have mostly left their hometowns to escape the famine. The emergency relief for the bandit area released by the Hubei Provincial Government has only received more than 3,000 yuan in Jianli. As a result of the distribution, each adult received only two mao, and each child received only one mao and a few cents. A family of five totaled less than one yuan. How could a cup of water help a cartload of firewood? The authorities must pay attention to it. At present, the organization of the security team and the volunteer team has begun to take shape. The security team is reorganized from the people's group with guns, and there are about 400 people. The volunteer team is organized by the strong men of the whole county, with a total of 176 large teams and more than 30,000 people. They are scattered in various villages, and training is not easy. In terms of military equipment, there are only spears and broadswords, and no guns. The Baojia system is currently being promoted. Each district has been budgeted and is sending people to compile and investigate. Before the bandit disaster, education in the county was not developed, and now it has completely gone bankrupt. There is still something to be done for reorganization and revitalization. The reporter arrived in Jianli with the inspection team at 8:00 am on the 13th. Due to the rush of time, they only stayed for about an hour before boarding the boat to Xindi. However, during this shortest time of inspection, witnessing the destruction of the towns and the suffering of the disaster victims, I felt shocked and could not help but sigh. On the way from Shashi to Jianli, on the night of the 12th, I stayed overnight in Tiaoxian, which belongs to Shishou County. The town is located on the south bank of the Yangtze River and is the main road for the communist bandits of Honghu to enter Hunan. It has been trampled by bandits several times, and the traces of destruction are everywhere. There is now a Xiang army stationed there. According to the locals, there are bandits lurking a dozen miles away from the town, and it remains to be cleared. (Sent from Xindi on December 15)

Record of the Inauguration of the New Fujian Provincial Committee

Cai Tingkai has also arrived at the Pacification Headquarters to assume his duties

Fuzhou Correspondence: The order for the reorganization of the Fujian Provincial Government was received by telegram from the Office of the Civil Secretary of the National Government on the 12th and reached Fujian. The provincial government immediately instructed all departments to expedite the closing of affairs to facilitate the handover. By the 14th, all departments had completed the handover procedures and the provincial government notified the newly appointed Chairman Jiang Guangnai to schedule the takeover. On the 15th, Jiang sent Mai Qian, Secretary of the Pacification Headquarters, to the provincial government to announce that the new committee members would arrive at the government office at 10:00 AM on the 16th to take their oath of office. On the 16th, merchants and residents throughout the city hung flags to celebrate. Around 9:00 AM, Jiang Guangnai, along with Li Zhangda, Fan Qiwu, Sun Xiwu, Lu Wenlan, and Lin Zhiyuan - five people in total (Zheng Zhenwen, Gao Dengting, and Li Qingquan had not yet arrived) - arrived at the provincial government in cars from the Pacification Headquarters. They were greeted by Guo Shihui, the Secretary-General of the Provincial Government, along with the heads of various sections. At 10:00 AM, the oath of office ceremony was held. Zhan Yuan, sent by the Central Government, served as the oath supervisor, and Wei Datong, sent by the National Government, announced the order. Many guests from various circles attended the ceremony. The ceremony concluded around 11:00 AM. Li Zhangda immediately went to the Secretariat, Fan Qiwu to the Finance Department, and Sun Xiwu to the Construction Department. Jiang Guangnai sent Qiu Yu to the Civil Affairs Department to take over their respective responsibilities, and announced the appointment of section chiefs, secretaries, and other important officials. From the provincial government side, there were Guo Le (former Secretary-General of the Provincial Government), Wang Hanqing (advisor), Yin Gongwu, Chen Zhonghe, and Lin Chi (former secretaries of the Provincial Government), Zhang Jingtang (former head of the Second Section of the Provincial Government) as the head of the First Section, Mai Qian as the head of the Second Section, Guo Boxiang as the head of the Third Section, and Jiang Yanken as the head of the Fourth Section. The new provincial government has scheduled to begin operations on the 17th and hold the first meeting of the Provincial Government Committee. It is heard that the Finance Department will first allocate one month's worth of funding to various agencies within one or two days to the Education Department, as the new director Zheng Zhenwen only arrived in Fujian from Shanghai on the Hua'an steamer on the 16th and is expected to take office on the 19th. However, the current Director, Cheng Shi, sealed the seals and handed them over to the provincial government on the evening of the 15th, ceasing operations and awaiting the takeover.

With the new Provincial Committee having taken office, the former Director of the Pacification Headquarters, Jiang Guangnai, has now been transferred to the position of Provincial Chairman. The Central Government has appointed Cai Tingkai to take over as the Director of the Pacification Headquarters. Cai arrived in Fuzhou by plane a few days ago and, after consulting with Jiang Guangnai and being urged by various parties, assumed his duties at the Pacification Headquarters on the 15th. He will schedule his oath of office at a later date. Cai has also formulated a plan to streamline the organization within the Pacification Headquarters and, in consultation with Jiang, has largely finalized issues such as personnel retention and expense reduction. It is expected that these measures will be gradually implemented in the coming days. (December 17th)

The Bankruptcy Case of Songjiang Bank

Peculiar Judgment by the County Court

Creditors Decide to Appeal

Songjiang Bank was founded in the first year of the Republic. In the 17th year, the president, Xie Zaiping, died of illness. His son, Xie Liangda, was appointed as president. The bank was not registered, but the organization adopted a corporate system. Therefore, the president, directors, and supervisors were all elected by the shareholders' meeting and were important officials in charge of business operations. At the end of January of this year, due to the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the market was closed. On February 5th, when the Shanghai branch went bankrupt, the president and supervisors withdrew six or seventy thousand yuan from the head office's inventory of over eighty thousand yuan. On the last page of the bank's cash flow book, it was recorded that the head office also ceased operations on the 10th, and the president fled without a trace. The total amount of overdue public and private deposits was over six hundred thousand yuan, posing a threat to the social financial system. The bank's directors petitioned the Songjiang County Government to organize a liquidation committee, which was composed of the original supervisors as liquidation committee members. The first meeting was held on February 23rd. On the 17th, over eleven thousand yuan of the inventory was paid back to Lu Jiji and other accounts. The creditors, therefore, distrusted the committee and filed civil and criminal lawsuits with the county court, as well as a request for evidence preservation. The court president, Wang, ordered officials to seal up the bank. The County Magistrate Shen repeatedly refused under the pretext of liquidation. By mid-April, the provincial government ordered the transfer of the bank's evidence to the court for handling. The court president, Wang, selected two accountants, Xi Yushu and Xia Sunhuan, to conduct the liquidation. In early August, one-tenth of the deposits were repaid, and evidence of destruction was discovered, such as cash receipts, cash payment receipts, transfer account receipts, remittance books, stub books, and inventory lists. Concealed assets such as bond coupons and provincial government bonds, railway stocks, etc., totaled over twenty thousand yuan, which flowed out of the bank's accounts. During the market closure on February 5th of this year, the total number of revenue and expenses reached more than 600,000 yuan, which is especially alarming. Furthermore, the handwriting and ink marks on the latest draft flow books are consistent throughout, without any discrepancies, which also raises suspicions. The civil suit portion of the case has been accepted and has been heard six times by October. In the fourth summons, 115 plaintiff creditors were summoned. In the fifth summons, due to the death of the defendant Zhang Shengshan, the court ordered the correction of the lawsuit. The legal heirs of Zhang Shengshan, Zhang Jitai and Zhang Jixiang, appointed lawyer Sha Xunyi as their agent. The final hearing was held on the sixth day, and the verdict was scheduled to be announced on December 12. On that day, the civil division publicly announced the main text of the case of Wu Boyang and 110 others versus Zhang Shengshan and others regarding deposit disputes. The plaintiff's request to withdraw the suit against the defendant Zhu Hesheng Gu Jiaxuan should be approved, and the rest should be considered withdrawn. The plaintiffs are responsible for the cost of litigation. Upon reading the document, the creditors were deeply surprised that the partial withdrawal of the suit affected the whole case. As for the criminal suit, after the prosecution was filed, the investigation took ten months and the court hearings were held three times. On December 19, the procuratorate delivered the disposition documents to the plaintiffs, two copies for each person. One copy was the indictment against Xie Liangda, the absconded bank manager, and the other was the non-prosecution disposition for the directors and warehouse keepers. However, the plaintiffs stated that there were some discrepancies in the factual aspects of the non-prosecution disposition document. Moreover, it was not mentioned that the directors, supervisors, and warehouse keepers of the bank recognized the absconding of the bank manager, all the acts of destroying evidence and concealing property were illegal and incomprehensible. It is now reported that the creditors' side is not satisfied with the court's judgment and intends to hold a meeting to discuss a unified response, decide to appeal and apply for a retrial, and have also submitted a request to the Ministry of Justice to thoroughly investigate to uphold the rule of law.

Nan Hui: Impersonating Officials to Claim Stolen Goods, Arrested and Escorted to the County

The Guanghua brand kerosene of the Shanghai Meida Company, carried by the Qiaji sailboat, was repeatedly stolen and intercepted in the sea area bordering Nan Hui and Feng Xian, and the case has been reported for investigation. Recently, hundreds of cans of kerosene were successively intercepted in the areas of Ni Cheng, Tangjiaozi, and in the Dongmen River of the city. The suspects Tang Guoxiang, Shao Genlian, and Jin Kaiyu were detained by the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Unexpectedly, Xi Youlin, nephew of Jin Guanxing, conceived a whimsical plan and led a Westerner, posing as the manager of the Madason Foreign Company, and false witnesses Cai Tiyi and Fang Fuchun, etc., chartered a small motorboat from Shanghai named "McCity" on the previous day, intending to impersonate the owner and claim the goods, and asked for the release of Jin Guanxing and others. The Director of the Public Security Bureau, Jin Runzhang, recognized them immediately and detained Xi Youlin, Cai Tiyi, Fang Fuchun, etc. One Westerner escaped. The bureau immediately escorted Jin Guanxing and others who had been previously arrested to the county for interrogation. The hundreds of cans of kerosene that were intercepted were claimed by the Meida Company, who sent personnel to Nan Hui yesterday.

Jia Ding: Robbery at a Dyeing Workshop near Humin Bridge

In Humin Bridge Town of this county, more than ten robbers dressed in cloth skirts and armed with weapons broke through the Pai Men of Lu Yuanxing Liangfang at midnight on the 20th and robbed more than 300 bolts of cloth and 27 yuan in cash. Nearby villagers heard the noise and fired guns to pursue the robbers, who fled towards the Shanghai-Taiyuan Motor Road, setting fire to the bolts of cloth along the way. They were not caught.

Wu Xi: Confiscation of a Large Batch of Japanese Watches

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of this county received a secret report the day before yesterday stating that Huaxingli, Hengdeli, Huadeli, and Hengdali watch companies on Tongyun Road had recently imported a large batch of Japanese watches and requested that personnel be dispatched to inspect them. After receiving the report, the association's Inspection Section Director Tu Lianfu, together with all inspectors, set out in groups, accompanied by Gu Liewu, the police chief of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau, to conduct the inspection. Three wooden boxes of Japanese watches and thirty-five large clocks were seized at Huaxingli, three wooden boxes of Japanese watches and twenty-two large clocks were seized at Hengdeli, eight large clocks and eleven small clocks were seized at Huadeli, and three small clocks were seized at Hengdali. All of them were immediately sealed and sent to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association for identification and disposal.

Prevalence of Diphtheria and Smallpox in the City

Since the beginning of winter, there has been little rain and snow, and the climate has been unusually dry. As a result, diphtheria and smallpox are rampant inside and outside the city. Young children of school age, whose parents do not know how to prevent them, have been infected and died in considerable numbers. According to investigations, the number of people dying from these diseases in a single day is around several dozen, especially in the area within half a mile north of the city's tax office. Within a few hours, four children died of this disease, and the severity of the situation is truly alarming.

Zhu Liangsheng, the owner of a fruit store on Xinfeng Street outside Zhongshan Gate in Wu Yi, hanged himself on a pine tree behind his house on the evening of the 19th due to high debts and urgent demands from creditors, which he could not meet. On the morning of the 20th, he was found by passersby and taken home for burial.

Due to irregularities in the election of provincial representatives in various sub-districts of the Second District of this county, which were reported by the First District, the supervisor Huang Ren took the ballots to the province for counting. The fraudulent district sub-divisions were declared invalid and the process of handling the incident should be reported to the Headquarters. Reporting Smoking Creates Unexpected Complications

Gao Xiang, the head of Gaodun Township in the Tenth District, filed a lawsuit with the county government the other day, accusing Chen Zubei of smoking opium. The county government ordered the police to arrest and interrogate Chen according to the law. Subsequently, the defendant Chen Zubei surrendered himself and confessed that he had already gone to the hospital to quit. Then Gao Xiang declared that he was willing to accompany Chen to Renji Hospital to verify the facts. Now, Gao Xiang suddenly accused Judge Wang Cheng of the High Court of secretly detaining him in a secret room on the 15th and interrogating him severely late at night, forcing him to sign and seal, which he refused, resulting in him being ordered to be driven out of the door by the bailiffs. Judge Wang Cheng, upon hearing this, believed that Gao's words were arbitrary and fabricated, and yesterday he ordered the bailiff Wu Bowen to go to Suzhou to report to the High Court and order Gao Xiang to be brought to court for questioning.

Chang Shu: Concubine Surnamed Wang Commits Suicide Due to Abuse

Wang Nianqu, a wealthy household living in Zhaixi, Dayi Bridge, moved to Xijing Bank in the city two years ago due to inconvenience in the countryside. Wang's wife, Zhang, had a son and a daughter. The son passed away two years ago, leaving a daughter. Because Wang had no son under his knee, he entrusted Wang Xueqing, who worked as a room attendant in a hotel, to introduce a former maidservant surnamed Wang as a concubine, named Wang Xiuan. Although her appearance was not outstanding, she was initially favored by Nianqu. However, the first wife was exceptionally fierce and did not allow her husband to sleep with the concubine. Before long, she ordered Xiuan to live alone in the upstairs attic and often beat her severely. Xiuan, unable to bear the abuse, had attempted suicide by drowning last year, but was rescued. The other day, Xiuan had another quarrel with Zhang. In a moment of anger, she went upstairs and hanged herself. It was not until the morning of the 20th that she was discovered. They immediately notified Xiuan's family. Xiuan's brother, Shunsheng, came to the city to deal with the matter. Wang, due to pressure from his father-in-law, did not dare to argue and only paid a hundred yuan to settle the matter.

Jia Xing: Police Detective Implicated in Kidnapping Case, Arrested

Changfu, the eldest son of Shi Ashui, a farmer from Shaoji Langjiaqiao in Kunlian, the sixth district of Xinghaiyan in Wangdian District, Jiaxing, was kidnapped by bandits on October 24. Five or six days later, he was murdered, and his body was weighted with stones and sunk in the Shenjiaqiao River in the northeast township of the fifth district (i.e., the first district of Wangdian). His corpse was later found floating, reported to the Jiaxing District Court for examination. Shi Ashui, because of the incident, dared not live in his village and moved to Daqiao Street in Wangdian East Town. He became acquainted with Guan Dexing, who claimed to be a detective in the sixth team of the Water Police, and observed that Guan's actions were suspicious. Guan repeatedly visited Shi's house before and after the kidnapping. However, due to lack of evidence, Shi did not dare to report him. Recently, the family of Zhong Ayang in Sangjiaqiao also received threatening letters. Ayang's son, Jinrong, went to Shanghai to negotiate, and Guan Dexing secretly followed him. Also, a similar incident happened to the family of Xia Jisheng. Guan had also revealed clues to Shi Ashui earlier. Therefore, Shi reported to the First A Baoan Tuan of Dongzhen in the Fifth District yesterday and had Guan arrested at the house of Yu Rongguan in Huanqiao Lane. The case was reported to the Haiyan County Government by telegram (because Haiyan had arrested a suspect). The Haiyan County Government sent Zhang Xiong, the police chief of the Shendang Public Security Bureau, along with police officers and four members of the Lianpu Temple Baoan Tuan, to Wangdian yesterday to bring the criminal to Salt for interrogation.

The Jiangdu County Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from Gu Xingyi of the Shanghai County Grain Association stating that the canal water was dry, and thousands of ships going up and down the river were blocked at Mapeng Bay. As the end of the year was approaching, the merchants were in great difficulty. All workers went on strike and stopped business operations. The two sides insisted on their positions. The County Public Security Bureau, upon hearing this, believed that transportation was very important during this winter defense period. Therefore, it sent the section chief of the bureau to mediate. It is now reported that the bureau has agreed to postpone the collection for ten days, while the workers will not allow collection until an order is received from the Department. The two sides are still in dispute.

Hangzhou: Younger Brother Kills Older Brother

Wu Fengqi of Dongyang, who ran a plastering business in Yanding Lane, Lianqiao, Hangzhou, had a younger brother, Fenglin, who helped his brother in his business. The business was doing well. On the morning of the ninth of this month, Fengqi asked his brother for money and was refused. He immediately took a bamboo knife and ran upstairs. While Fengqi was still in bed, he stabbed him four times, twice in the head. Because Fenglin woke up and resisted with his feet, his left and right knees were also stabbed once each. At that time, Fenglin was still able to support himself and chased Fengqi to Lianqiao, where he caught Fengqi and sent him to the First District Seventh Branch of the Public Security Bureau for questioning and detention. He was later released on bail. After Fenglin was injured, the two wounds to his head were light, but the wounds to his knees were deep and wide. Because the treatment was not proper, his thighs became swollen and festered. He died of his injuries the other day. His brother, Fengqi, fled without a trace upon hearing the news. The Hangzhou County Court Procuratorate received the report and dispatched Prosecutor Zhao Zhisui and examiner Feng Shengxiang to Lezhu in Saozhou Bay, Jianggan, yesterday morning (21st) to perform an autopsy on the corpse. It was determined that Wu Fengqi had died of his injuries. They filled out an injury report and reported it to the court, and at the same time ordered the guarantor to hand over the murderer for punishment. It is reported that the murderer Wu Fengqi has been found in Lin'an County by the guarantor and will be escorted to Hangzhou for interrogation.

The City Government's Six Million Public Bonds Sell Well

Exceeding the Original Amount by 1.78 Million Yuan in Two Hours of Public Sale Yesterday

The City Government's six million yuan Recovery Public Bonds were fully underwritten by Liyan Foreign Company.
