Recent Tianjin Yarn and Cotton Market Report

Organized Cotton Remains Flat (19th) Tianjin report: The market situation for organized cotton in Xihai remains flat. Western firms bought 261 bales, offered at 23.5 taels. The Yu Ji firm of the Shanghai guild bought 1,200 bales at 23.4 taels. Foreign firms completed 620 bales, the price remained at 23.4 taels.

American Upland Cotton Jumps Up Tianjin report of the same day: American Upland cotton in Xihai is still being purchased with vigor from all sides, showing significant improvement. The Yu Ji firm of the Shanghai guild actually bought 790 bales, offered at 29.5 taels, and another 50 bales at 29 taels.

Donghai Long-staple Cotton Firmly Rises Tianjin report of the same day: The Donghai long-staple cotton market is active, and prices have risen again. The Yu Ji firm of the Shanghai guild bought 200 bales, offered at 29.5 taels, an increase of 0.1 tael.

Cotton Yarn Consumption Quiet Tianjin report of the same day: The local cotton yarn trade remains sluggish, and the atmosphere is peaceful. Only the Baigou guild bought 10 bundles of Blue Tiger yarn at 114.5 taels.

Grains and Flour Prices Surge Uniformly

Yesterday, the flour market continued to be brisk, and the market was extremely tight. Futures prices for all goods rose uniformly. Spot flour was extremely scarce, and factories had already raised prices to 2.05 taels, with no large quantities available. Delivery of completed orders was being pushed to January and February. Customers were still actively seeking goods. The mid- to long-term market saw fierce competition between bulls and bears, leading to an unexpected surge. At the opening of the market in the morning, foreign wheat was quoted slightly lower, at 0.2 taels. Canadian wheat was traded at 2,000 tons at a price of 3.5 taels. Australian wheat from Nanjing was not negotiated for at a price of 3.4 taels. At that time, the mood was calm and prices were soft. In the afternoon, gold prices rose, and foreign wheat was in demand by both local and outside customers. Prices for all months soared uniformly. Before the close, the surge became even more frantic. The current month's price was nearly 2 taels higher. The closing prices were: current month up 1.75 taels, January up 3.25 taels, February up 3.5 taels, March up 3 taels, April up 3.5 taels, and May up 3 taels.

Fujian Guild Continues to Purchase Kehsien Rice

| Foreign Rice Stock at 440,000 Bags |

Yesterday, the Fujian guild had an active appetite for Kehsien rice. Local traders were willing to sell, but because river rice could be re-exported and was cheaper, they shifted their attention to that. Trading in Kehsien rice was temporarily on hold. However, the Fujian guild was not interested in river rice and focused on Kehsien and Keyuan rice. Yesterday, they bought 408 bags of Wuhu machine-milled rice at prices ranging from 9.65 to 9.40 taels, 300 bags of Hunan machine-milled rice at 8.10 taels, and 200 bags of machine-milled oil rice at 8.62 taels. The market situation was similar to the previous day. Red rice was purchased by Quanzhou, while the rest was purchased by Fuzhou. The rice inventory stored in Shanghai was 445,000 bags, all owned by the British firms Jardine Matheson and Ewo. The floating supply on the market had been exhausted, so there were no sales.

Chicago Wheat Continues to Weaken

On Tuesday (20th), Chicago wheat initially fell due to weakness in the Liverpool market, but then rose due to purchases from the East. The total trading volume on the 19th was 10 million bushels. The daily market prices are listed below:

Closing Price Compared to Previous Day

Sugar Market, Domestic Raw Sugar Market Both Weak

Yesterday, the sugar market was quite active in trading, and the trend was firm. In the morning, Changxing offered 1,400 bags of Grade 24 white sugar at 15.5 taels. In the afternoon, the guild made a good offer of 0.05 taels, at 15.55 taels, but the traders did not bite, resulting in no transactions. Eight hundred oil bags of Dutch red sugar were offered, priced at 11.5 taels. The Xinchao Raw Sugar firm continued to offer goods, with a total of 600-700 bags traded at prices ranging from 8.85 to 8.5 taels, only 0.05 taels higher or lower than on the 13th, and the trend was stable. Due to the relatively large inventory of slab sugar and lower market prices, the price was 8.2-8.3 taels. Brick sugar trading was limited, with prices around 8 taels. The Xinzhang firm's offer and bid prices did not align, so no transactions were made. However, the market outlook is not good, and long-term inaction will hinder the source market.

Also received a New York sugar market report: spot prices are still calculated at 8.125 cents per pound, futures prices are up 3 points for December/May, down 1 point for January, up 2 points for March, and up 1 point for July/September. The London and Java sugar markets remain unchanged.

Hardware, Sesame Nails Fixed at 1,000 Boxes

Yesterday's London telegram: The fixed price for sesame nails is 31 shillings per box, with 1,000 boxes made. It is said that this transaction was handled by the firms of Ward and Yongxing.

Hardware Merchants Head North in Succession

Recently, the weather has gradually turned cold, and the northern ports are freezing, so the shipment of hardware to Tianjin, Yantai, and other ports in the north is decreasing daily. Moreover, with the approaching end of the year, merchants from various ports are preparing to wrap up business. Therefore, there are several instances each day of merchants packing up and heading north. As for the merchants from Sichuan and other areas upstream along the Yangtze River, the river is drying up, and frequent warfare makes trading difficult, so many are also returning west. Therefore, recent trading in the local market, except for manufacturers making small adjustments, large-scale transactions are as rare as morning stars.

Free Talk

Lotus Drop (3)

— Mu Shiying

He cried again, and after crying for a while, said, "What am I going to do?"

"Let's go together!"

So we walked south together, not knowing where we were going. She didn't say anything on the road, and I didn't dare to say anything either. When we arrived at a town, she said, "I'm really hungry." So I ran to a pancake shop and begged the shopkeeper, "Sir, have pity on me, I'm starving. The house was ransacked by soldiers, and I've been running for a day and a night without anything to eat." The shopkeeper acted as if he didn't hear me. I had no choice but to walk away. She was standing at the corner, waiting for me with a reproachful look on her face. I had no choice but to walk in front of a silk shop, and for some reason, I thought of Lotus Drop, so I lowered my head and sang: "Oh dear! The plum blossoms are blooming and falling, one plum blossom at a time! Winter plum blossoms!"

I felt my face turning red, and there were many people around me watching. I really wanted to disappear into the ground. At this moment, I suddenly heard someone singing along with me. I looked and saw it was her. I don't know where she got two broken bamboo pieces, which she held in her hand, tapping them rhythmically. I became emboldened, immediately straightened my chest, raised my head, and sang the Lotus Drop loudly. We were two people singing together.

From that day on, we wandered like autumn leaves, from this city to that city. Later, we also got a broken huqin (Chinese violin), so with a huqin and a clapper, together, over one mountain after another, over one river after another, in front of the thatched cottage's wooden door, in front of the black lacquered gate, we sang the Lotus Drop.

Last night, we were sitting in a small alley. She was feeling a little feverish, leaning against me, and looked at my hair and said, "Your hair is a bit gray too."

"Isn't it? I'm over forty years old, how can my hair not be white?"

"It's been over twenty years, almost thirty years, since we ran out of the pavilion. Time really flies! Do you remember, one year we were in Henan, and we didn't get anything to eat for three days? You were so angry at that time that you hit me for no reason, and you bruised my waist a lot! Do you remember?"

"Didn't you scratch my face too?"

"Wasn't that night in the pavilion very much like tonight?"

I raised my head: there was a crescent moon in the eaves, turning all the black tiles into silver.

"But I'm really tired!" She leaned her head on my shoulder, it was so heavy.

I didn't pay attention. I just kept looking at the moon. But she just died like that.

With a clapper and a huqin, together, over one river after another, over one mountain after another, in front of the thatched cottage's wooden door, in front of the black lacquered gate, in the street, in the wheat field, we sang the Lotus Drop together. We laughed together, cried together, sighed together, and wiped away tears together: there was a me in this world, and there was a her! We were two people.

Yes, we were two people, but she died last night. (The End)

On the Selection of Novels

— Xie Liuyi

(I selected a) "Model Novel" for a certain bookstore in Shanghai in the first half of the year. Each chapter has an analytical introduction. This article is intended to be used as a preface to the original book. It is now published in advance here, just to correct "Dayi One."

In the past, Jin Shengtan commented on Water Margin, commenting on the place where Pan Jinlian called Wu Song "Uncle, Uncle." Shengtan started counting from the first time she called out "Uncle," and counted all the way to more than thirty. The final comment was, "Writing about a lewd woman is like writing about a living lewd woman. After calling 'Uncle' thirty-nine times, she suddenly changes to using the word 'you,' which is a wonderful thought and a wonderful pen." This kind of appreciative criticism, in China, where there is not much achievement in literary criticism, still has considerable value even today. Although there are now criticisms of the "vague consciousness" type, such as "being able to grasp reality," I am afraid to say that overly general criticisms are not good. There is a writer in China who once asserted in a magazine that the young people of our country no longer write classical Chinese. Of course, this is what we have been hoping for. Articles like "Heaven and earth are the universe, and my heart truly embraces it. It has been a long time, not just a day for a hundred years..." or "Your Majesty, I have heard that those who seek the growth of trees must first..." We, standing on the principles of evolution, certainly do not believe that young people today are willing to pick up a pen and write such articles. Isn't the era moving forward? However, the fact has already proved that they cannot write the old eight-legged essays, but they are quite good at writing new eight-legged essays. For example, to describe the meaning of "many," some people, no matter where, when, or in what article, always cannot help but use the phrase "like bamboo shoots after a rain"; they always use the phrase "everything, everything" to summarize things; to explain the depth of an impression, they always use the sentence "forever engraved in the heart" in any article. My exposing this is very much suspected of "nitpicking." In the eyes of those who claim to be revolutionaries, words are of secondary importance, and the most important thing is "correct consciousness" and "upholding the interests of one's own class." However, I think that there is too much new eight-legged essay writing, which may hinder the "correctness of consciousness" and may even reduce the power of "upholding the interests of one's own class." Our hope is very simple, not only for everyone to have "correct consciousness" and "be able to uphold the interests of one's own class," but also to hope that everyone will write fewer new eight-legged essays. Do not blindly imitate others, but be able to self-reflect and create new words.

Everyone can appreciate the works of others, as long as they recognize the words. There is no need to analyze other people's works. Anyway, after reading it once, if the original work is good, just praise it with a sentence like "detailed description"; if the original work is not good, just scold it with a sentence like "written in a confused manner." It is a clever method to leave things unfinished in the world. Even if you want to take a work to analyze and explain its merits and demerits, everyone has their own views, and it is really difficult to force others to be the same as oneself, and it is absolutely impossible to be uniform. I don't want to be a "guidepost," my highest goal is just to write down the slightest gains from my personal appreciation of works and provide them to young people who like to read novels: to help them in terms of "words," "consciousness," and "description."

Opening the dictionaries of Chinese writers published in the market, there are almost enough Chinese writers to make up the number of five hundred Han people. But I only selected the works of five writers in this book. I have long braced myself and prepared for other writers to beat me and scold me. And I have already guessed the first sentence that will scold me. This sentence that scolds me is none other than "Are you short-sighted!" In fact, my eyes are not short-sighted, and I have also used binoculars to look around in this desert area. There are definitely more than five writers in China, this is a true and certain fact. However, what I am doing is the work of a "craftsman." When a craftsman chooses materials, he must consider whether they can fit his own "ink line." As a result of my selection, the works of these five writers can fit my ink line, so I am going to presume upon their works. As for the other masterpieces of other writers, let other craftsmen use them. (December 17)

The Swiss Girl

— Liu Feng

The scenery of Switzerland, even for those who have not personally traveled there, cannot help but be fascinated by thinking about it or hearing about it; but does Switzerland have nothing else to captivate people besides the white snow of the Alps and the green waves of Lake Lucerne? Ah, no. This peaceful and quiet country, in addition to her bright mountain scenery and water colors that are everywhere, also has the strongest, most beautiful, and most romantic women who make travelers fall in love.

Swiss women are very romantic before marriage. What Chinese people call "romantic affairs" are almost universal in Switzerland. This magazine published an article by Mr. Wan Ju on the 5th of this month entitled "The Swiss Girl." Here are two additional stories based on what I have seen and heard.

A farmer in a certain place in Switzerland was always lamenting that the fruits in his orchard were being stolen; one day, a foreign tourist heard him lamenting like this and asked him, "Why don't you raise a dog?" The honest farmer replied, "Then my daughters will never be able to marry." The foreigner was a little confused when he heard him say this, and asked him what he meant. He replied, "I used to raise a dog, which was very ferocious. Whenever it saw someone coming to my house, it would bark wildly, and as a result, a group of young people dared not come to peep through the windows of our house anymore."

There is also a village chief in a rural village, who is one of the most respected gentlemen in the local area. He often praised his woman to the people he knew. He said very proudly, "When my woman was young, no woman could compare to her, because she had the most 'Kelter'!" What this means is that no woman could spend the night with as many men as his wife. It turns out that in some parts of Switzerland, unmarried girls often spend the night with their lovers without any restraint on Saturday nights, and no one finds it strange at all.

Statistics on Suicide

— Qing Hao

"Suicide" is so terrible, but in this world, there are many people who commit suicide. Could it be that they are tired of living?

Here are some statistics on suicide: According to the statistics of the New York Life Insurance Company, more than 20,000 Americans committed suicide last year, that is, 20 people out of every 100,000 people committed suicide. In 1915, it accounted for 20.8, and in 1908, it accounted for 21.5. The capital of Wisconsin Province has a population of 58,000, and its suicide rate is 44.8.

According to the statistics of the New York Department of Health, there were 1,500 suicides in New York last year, an increase of 97 people compared with 1930. Three-quarters of them committed suicide using the following methods:

Tool Male Female

Poisonous gas 408 169

Hanging 152 22

Jumping off a building 93 9

Handgun 89 4

Poison 66 56

Knives 47 5

According to a survey released by the German Bureau of Statistics, the number of suicides last year reached 18,000, that is, at least 30 people out of every 100,000 people committed suicide. In the first four months of 1932 alone, the number of suicides in Berlin reached 700. Japan is militaristic and its economic panic is more severe than that of other countries, so the number of suicides is also higher than that of other countries. According to the Cabinet Bureau of Statistics, the average number of suicides in Japan is 58 per day. From January to April this year, there were 694 suicides, of which women accounted for one-third, and most of them were between 21 and 25 years old.

New Scientific Weapons (3)

— Yi

The third type of terrifying new weapon is the killing ray and the strangeness ray. These two rays were already making a lot of noise in the world at the end of the Great War. Later, France's Heraclius, Italy's Verifi, and Britain's Matthews all devoted themselves to studying the effectiveness of this ray, which can injure people and horses, prevent the operation of tanks and airplanes, and cause long-distance gunpowder depots to explode suddenly. If these two rays are once used as new weapons, then all modern military equipment will completely lose its value. But most people in the world do not believe in the effectiveness of these two rays. They say that this is nothing more than "bragging or" "a fable."

In fact, these two rays are both composed of extremely short radio waves, which is a credible fact. Whether it is a person or a horse, when touched by this ray, a strong heating effect will occur in its organs or cells, and the severity of the injury will vary depending on the length of the "wavelength" touched. This has been tested on animals and is very accurate. Therefore, these two rays are recognized as new weapons. Other weapons, such as dazzling rays, killing rays, and killing sound waves, are also monsters on future military equipment, which can be mentioned in passing here. Killing sound waves were discovered by Professors Wood and Lewis of Johns Hopkins University in the United States. A special electrical machine is used to increase the frequency of radio waves to 100,000 to several hundred thousand vibrations per second, and then these sound waves are used to kill several people. This high-frequency sound wave cannot be heard by the ear and is called "silent sound wave." Animals that are vibrated by this sound wave die in a state of dementia.

According to the opinions expressed by the discoverers, this sound wave causes the death of the organism because it resonates with the various cell tissues of the organism. The discoverers have tested fish and frogs in the water and have obtained the same effect. The above-mentioned new weapons, such as killing rays, strangeness rays, and killing sound waves, require a very large power supply during manufacture, and their effective range is very narrow. Therefore, they have not been actually used as weapons until now. Perhaps they will be used in general battles after further research.

The above are the weapons used in battle. In addition, there are several electrical security weapons. First, let's talk about the electrical eye. This is also a kind of ray that cannot be seen with the naked eye. Its electrical nerves are distributed everywhere and are all connected. For example, in coastal fortresses, artillery pieces are set up everywhere, and electrical eyes are set up to connect with each other. As long as an enemy ship is found in one place, all the artillery pieces can be concentrated to fire, so that the enemy ship can be sunk in an instant.

Secondly, there is the electrical ear. The highest and lowest sound waves cannot be heard by human ears (sound waves with a frequency of less than 20 and more than 20,000 vibrations per second cannot be heard by human ears), but the electrical ear can hear them. The party equipped with the electrical ear can detect all the enemy's arrangements, even if the enemy has a silencing device. It can detect the enemy's location or notify friendly forces to report that the attack has begun. In addition, high-frequency sound waves have strong directivity (that is, the property of advancing in a certain direction) and reflectivity, so they can also be used to detect enemy ships that cannot be seen with the naked eye during night sea battles, and they can also measure the distance and bombard them fiercely.

In the future, electricity will dominate the world of weapons. Compared with future electrical weapons, the current poisonous gas, tanks, and airships are far behind. The progress of scientific weapons may lead to the discovery of weapons that can annihilate all of humanity. The discovery of such weapons will probably be the time when war is abolished.

Zeppelin's Achievements

The German airship "Zeppelin" has made a total of 290 flights since its birth, passing through 536,600 kilometers and spending a total of 5,369 hours in flight, up to its return to Friedrichshafen on November 3 this year. Therefore, in terms of its speed, it is about 100 kilometers per hour (one kilometer is equivalent to one and two-thirds Chinese miles). It has carried a total of 7,495 passengers. If only this year is considered, then from the beginning of January 1 this year to November 3, it has made a total of 58 flights, with a flight time of 1,766 hours, a distance of 187,788 miles, a total of 1,218 passengers carried, and 2,745 kilograms of mail carried (one kilogram is more than two pounds), or one million letters. The total amount of goods transported is about 2,000 kilograms. Since its birth, it has traveled back and forth to South America a total of 13 times, five of which reached Livorno.

Long Creative Novel

The Long Creative Era and the Crossroads of Love, Part 22

— Zhang Ziping

Cao Shiguang held up three fingers. "So, after deducting the travel expenses, there's not much left."

"Still isn't it?"

Lin Haiquan knew that this fellow villager was an extremely romantic young man. After entering C University, he studied and pursued love simultaneously. Because he suffered from an indiscriminate eating disorder and only sought cheapness regardless of quality, one of his friends, surnamed Duan, pushed a girlfriend he couldn't handle onto him. According to fellow villagers, that woman was already pregnant with Duan's child.

The woman's name was Li Huiying. Sure enough, after living in the same building as Cao Shiguang for more than seven months, she gave birth to a baby girl. Now, Cao Shiguang was studying and managing household affairs simultaneously. From Haiquan's perspective, his recent life was indeed bleak and pitiable.

"Old Lin, shall I introduce you to the church?" "What are the benefits?" Haiquan asked with a smile.

"Believing in religion is not about benefits." "Forget it." Haiquan looked at Shiguang's feigned seriousness and laughed.

"There are many genuine articles, and they are all from decent families." "Have you made any progress?" "I regret it now. What can I do?" Cao Shiguang shook his head and sighed.

Seeing the bus approaching, "Let's go," Shiguang pulled at Haiquan's sleeve. "Where to?" "I'll introduce you to Pastor Habar. There's a prayer meeting at five o'clock today. After the prayer meeting, that old foreigner will definitely treat us to dinner."

Haiquan was originally a modern university student, going through the motions, with nothing to do after class. He didn't have a specific purpose for coming out today. With Cao Shiguang's pull, he got on the bus. The ticket seller came to them.

"Where to?" "Where to?" Haiquan was busy counting copper coins, and as he counted, he turned to ask Cao Shiguang. "H Road Intersection... I have copper coins, let me pay." As Shiguang spoke, he reached into his semi-old Western-style suit pocket and rummaged around. After a moment, he still hadn't managed to find any coins. Haiquan had already counted out the fare for both of them.

Talks

Seeking Work for the People

— Tianfang

According to a 국민신문 [probably an error in the original] report from Berlin on the 15th, German Chancellor Schleicher said in a radio address that the policy of the government, in a word, is to seek work for the people. The people's urgent need is in this. As for amending the constitution and other good things that cannot stop hunger, they are not what the government wants. Only the revival of commerce can end the panic of unemployment. But to comfort the people with empty words, saying that after lean years, there will be good years, is really useless. Therefore, the cabinet is now drafting a great plan to seek work for the people.

This is indeed the urgent task of rulers in all countries, because in the modern capitalist way of life, on the one hand, there is a surplus of people, and the number of unemployed worldwide has exceeded 30 million. China has no statistics, but 100 million is probably not far off. On the other hand, goods are discarded on the ground, machines are idle, wheat is dumped into the water, and fields are restricted from planting. These kinds of contradictory phenomena cannot be improved until the entire economic system is thoroughly reformed.

Since the Great War, Germany has suffered from the burden of reparations, the loss of markets, the increase in the number of unemployed, and financial bankruptcy. The country was almost no longer a country. But the Germans still have the characteristics of Germans, with copper and iron bodies and steel-like will. Finally, the Rhineland was evacuated, invited into the League of Nations, and the reparations plan was revised. The national power is flourishing, making France uneasy in bed. Recently, it has continued to train young people extremely, advocating the restoration of conscription and demanding equal military power, making the countries of Western Europe uneasy. A depleted ball has actually inflated. This is not a miracle, but the result of ten years of struggle by the entire German people. Seeing other people's efforts really makes our uncompetitive nation feel ashamed.

In theory, two or three people have the same two hands and two feet, a brain, and bear the same responsibility to society. Who can not drink and eat, then who can not work? But in the current society, "eating family property" is still a noun, and "eating ability" has not yet become widespread. The authorities have no time to ask if you have food and clothing, if you have work. The government is always crying poverty, but the land has not been fully utilized, things have not been fully used, and people have not been fully utilized. In the current society, some people are idle and have nothing to do, and some people have work but it is equivalent to nothing. Workers are working all day long, and they are still worried that they will not catch a cold and fever when they sleep at night. Once the children increase, the farmers sow and weed, and work hard all year round, they are still worried about whether there will be new year's food this year. Life is so insecure, how can society have vitality? Therefore, those who do not have work should be given work, and those who already have work must be guaranteed the stability of their lives.

Wine

— Leng Mei

The alcohol content of wine varies. Among the famous wines of various countries, the alcohol content of Portuguese Port wine is the highest, ranging from 14 to 24%. Spanish Sherry is second, about 16 to 18%. Italian Marsala contains 16%. French Burgundy contains 10.5%. German Rhine wine contains the least, 10.2%.

The method of making wine is to place fresh grape juice in a fermentation barrel for fermentation. Because there is always a grape sugar enzyme in the air that can freely parasitize in fresh grape juice, it reproduces very quickly, thus naturally fermenting. The temperature during fermentation should be maintained at 10 to 12 degrees. The fermentation barrel used is not covered, because a small amount of air is needed. (Excessive air contact can easily cause acetic acid bacteria in the grape juice, causing the wine to turn sour, which should be noted.) After 15 days, divide it into bottles, without tightly covering them. Wait for fermentation for several months, until the sugar content is completely converted into alcohol, clarified, and poured into wooden barrels. Tightly cover and store in a cold cellar until the wine matures, with a special aroma. This aroma is caused by the combination of the fragrant substances contained in the grape juice and the various alcohols and organic acids contained in the wine to form organic esters. When wine becomes moldy, it can make the color fade and have a bad smell, so it must be disinfected. Use a disinfection method to boil the wine bottle in 60 degrees hot water to kill the various microorganisms attached to it, but the temperature used should not be too high to prevent damage to the wine taste. Adding alcohol to the wine can also make the wine more stable and have stronger antibacterial properties.

High-quality wine does not add chemicals. For ordinary wine, if it is weak, you can add stronger wine. If it is sour, you can add invert sugar to supplement it. If you think it is light, you can add glycerin to thicken it. These can make up for the various shortcomings of the wine made.

The brandy that is currently popular on the market can also be distilled from already brewed wine. This kind of distilled clear liquid contains about 45% to 55% alcohol. It must be stored in wooden barrels made of oak, and it will gradually turn light yellow over time, with a special wine taste.

There is a wine called Champagne, which is also made from grapes. This wine is richest in France, containing 8.4 to 9.8% alcohol.

The method of making it is to first place the best quality grape juice in a barrel. After the dregs have completely settled to the bottom, (about 24 to 36 hours), inject the clarified liquid into a fermentation barrel. After fermentation for 15 days, change it to a tightly covered bottle, add a little brandy. Add a small amount of fish glue in winter, and add it again in February. In May, add 2% sucrose syrup and an appropriate amount of distiller's yeast, and then bottle and tighten it. Ferment it for 24 hours, place it on a bottle bed, and let it sit for about one to two years. At the summer solstice, the yeast residue gradually settles down. In winter, cool the bottle, invert it, and shake it, so that the yeast residue is attached to the cork. Quickly open the cork, and the yeast residue will naturally shoot out. Then quickly add the sugared brandy, replace the new cork, and tie it tightly with iron wire, so that the sugar content is completely fermented into carbon dioxide and alcohol. This type of wine is called dry sparkling wine. If the sugar content in the wine is not completely fermented and has stopped, the wine obtained is called sweet sparkling wine, which is not as palatable as dry sparkling wine.

Lamenting the Broken Walls and Ruins of Wusong

— Fu

This year, my close friends Xiaoxiao and Hangfu are studying in a school in Wusong. Our old friendship makes us often think of each other, so I invited a few friends to go to Wusong.

Our group of three, on a drizzly morning, jumped on the first steam train at Baoshan Road Station. The train dragged on unusually slowly, which gave us an opportunity to appreciate the scenery along the way. Along the way, there are scenes that are not easy to see, not forests, not lakes and mountains, not towering buildings, and not small thatched huts. On both sides of the tracks are piles of rubble, the remaining outlines of tall buildings. We quietly appreciate, appreciate the scenery after this great destruction. It is also shameful to say that we were not excited, nor were we indignant. We just silently watched on one side and listened on the other.

Listening to a person wearing a tattered Zhongshan suit giving instructions in a loud voice, he seemed to sympathize with our unfamiliarity, so he kept instructing us: "This is Fudan University, this is Chi-Zhi University, this is Labor University..." And constantly sighed with emotion, we all felt a little sad, and I especially felt the sadness of disillusionment: Our dignified universities have only these fragmented broken facades left! Alas!

When the train arrived in Wusong, we hired three "chartered" rickshaws and asked them to pull us to that ×× University where our friends were. The rickshaw pullers seemed particularly eager to please when they heard this, and ran like they were flying. They probably thought we were students here, and students are naturally regarded as the privileged class! The three of them ran desperately for a while and dragged the three of us to that place.

×× University was one that survived the fierce artillery fire and was spared from destruction. It is said that many parts were also bombed, but they have now been repaired. Looking closely, there are indeed still traces of scars all over the body. Xiaoxiao and Hangfu very diligently accompanied us to stroll around their school for a few laps. In the outer room of the gymnasium, I saw three commemorative bronze tablets. One of the people commemorated was our "national" person, and the other two were Germans, Paulun and Peruns. So, I thought: The fact that our "national" university was able to escape complete destruction, isn't it still thanks to the grace of these old gentlemen? Isn't the significance of this commemoration just in their achievements in running "this school"?

Our team has increased from three to five. The five of us, drinking mouthfuls of the northwest wind, walked along the beach. The earth mounds on the beach, piles of them, were sometimes high and sometimes low, some large and some small, some oval and some rectangular. It is said that these are trenches. There are also some caused by bursting shells. There are no houses on the beach anymore. In the ruins, you can still find the signs of a few hotels. We kept walking until we reached the front of the fort, and saw the "only" two machine gun-like gun muzzles, proudly watching south. We wanted to go closer to see, but we were stopped by a wooden sign that said "By order, no visitors allowed, Fort Manager Bai." Moreover, there were also barbed wire fences in front, and soldiers standing upright with bayonets on their rifles! I don't know why, but I wasn't afraid of this person with a bayonet, but felt very sorry for him. I thought that the sea and land winds blowing from all directions must be enough for him to drink? We stood under the fort, everyone thinking about this place two hundred and several ten days ago, and everyone seemed to have a feeling of lamenting the ancient battlefield.

We walked to the market street. The market street has a completely new atmosphere! Not a single one of the dozens of shops in the city is not painted bright yellow and green. The narrow streets are filled with the fragrance of tung oil and lime. This market street is the same as my hometown, so I feel like I have returned to my hometown. Moreover, this summer, a big fire broke out on the most bustling street in my hometown, extending a long street. It has now been rebuilt, and the entire street is also filled with tung oil and lime. There is construction only after destruction, so we have a custom in our hometown that after a fire, we must first thank the Fire God, probably because he promoted us to build! So, when I saw the brand-new atmosphere of Wusong Town after its reconstruction, I felt happy and deeply thought that we should first face east and thank him, thank him for giving us destruction!

The Female Gigolo in the Train Carriage

— Hongshui

For official business, I hurriedly boarded the train. Originally, I remembered that whenever I returned to my hometown for private matters, because I was short of copper coins, I had to spend that uncomfortable travel life in the fourth-class carriage, which was full of local smells and bad tastes. But now, I have completely lost my composure. Around me are couples of lovers, and gusts of fragrant aromas are constantly floating in the wind. There are also those few well-fed, snow-white, chubby gentlemen with lucky faces. That's right, with a "pass" for a first-class ticket, I can have this kind of enjoyment. The wheels were moving. At this time, a beautiful young woman, as beautiful as a flower and as radiant as jade, had filled my seat opposite me: Amidst a burst of laughter, the train left Shanghai far behind.

"Hello! Lend me a match." She said to me with a seductive, crisp smile.

"Okay." Naturally, I should hand her the whole box. In that instant, my soul began to shake. I thought embarrassedly; Could it be that fools have foolish luck? Could it be that I have encountered a stroke of good luck in love? Really, I took this opportunity to chat with her very warmly and happily.

"Where is your home?"

"Suzhou; Judging by your accent, madam, your home is probably in Nanjing, right?"

"Yes, my home is at No. ×, Zhongzheng Street. Please come and talk whenever you have the chance. Where are you going now?" "I have some miscellaneous matters, and I am also going to Nanjing." "Oh! How coincidental, let's go together. You can stop by my house for a rest when you get off the train."

"No, no, I'm sorry, because I have to go to the ×× Department right away."

"Don't you have any time to rest?" "This time, I am really in a hurry to discuss business matters, so I will have to visit you another time."

"What kind of business are you discussing?" "It's about the funds in the company." "Hahaha, yes, yes, then let's not be polite!" Her laughter was even more mixed, simply laughing so much that people couldn't bear it! We talked, leaning against the train window, admiring the beauty of nature. Another hometown—Suzhou—had arrived, ah, the poetic ancient city.

As usual, the train stopped at the station, and many travelers were squeezing on and off.

"I've also been to Beisi Pagoda, hey, that time I walked to the top of the pagoda, looked far and looked down, it almost scared me to death, haha." She pointed to the pagoda and said: "Ah, ah! My hat fell off at the station, I..."

"Okay, okay, I'll pick it up, you watch out here."

"Thank you!"

"Where is she? Oh, and my wallet?"

When I picked up the hat and found that she was not in her seat, I couldn't help but shout.

"Sir, be careful, there are many female gigolos on the train!" That weird tea boy laughed at me coldly.

Alas! The ruthless train was still moving forward!

Jiangbei Woman and Modern Woman

— Shiben

The day before yesterday, I took a long-distance bus to Shanghai in Minhang. When I bought the ticket and walked into the carriage, I saw that it was already crowded and there were no seats left. I knew that I had come too late and lost the right to sit. I had to stand hanging on the leather strap. But at that time, there were still fifteen minutes before the departure time, so there were still passengers who came after me. I only saw two Jiangbei women wearing blue cloth shirts, large silver coins hanging from their ears, and small, petite feet, also looking flustered, hurriedly running onto the carriage. Seeing this crowded scene, both of their faces immediately showed a state of uneasiness, and they looked at each other and said: "Oh dear! It's going to kill people! There are no seats left!" While saying this, they squeezed in straight through the crowd, hoping to find a seat, but it was already impossible. They had to learn my method, hanging on the leather strap like they were committing suicide.

Standing in front of the two Jiangbei women was a modern young man in a Western suit. I saw that his face showed displeasure, and he glared at them from time to time, as if blaming them for not coming in, making him annoyed, and even more for not knowing their place and standing in front of his new self, lest they touch his beautiful Western suit and infect him with the dirty, sour, and poor air of the Jiangbei women. I thought this modern young man was bound to lose his temper, but I knew it was not so. I only saw that not only did he not hate them, but he was also enthusiastically and kindly planning a way out for them, and said to them: "It's not good for you to sit here. Another one will open later. It's better to sit in the back," The two Jiangbei women listened and replied: "Sir, we asked. The one in the back will open at two o'clock! We still have to wait an hour," After saying this, they didn't seem to think the modern young man's words were right, and they still stood still. He heard this and hurriedly said: "Don't misunderstand, this one (pointing to the one he was sitting in) will also open at two o'clock. It will open at the same time as the one in the back!" When he said this, the two of them became happy, thinking that if they opened at two o'clock the same way, they would be happy to sit in the empty car in the back, how comfortable it would be, so they smiled and hurried to get off the bus. When the women got off the bus, I only heard him say to himself: "Annoying! She's getting a free ride."

The ticket had already been punched, and the bus was about to leave in three minutes. I knew that there was still a beautiful modern woman coming up. As soon as she got on the bus, her fragrance of clothes and flesh shone in all directions, attracting everyone in the car to pay attention to her. Seeing the appearance of "full of passengers", she turned her head and said to herself: "So many people! It's not easy to sit. I'll go to the one in the back," After saying this, she turned around and wanted to get off the bus. I only saw the modern young man who had just told the Jiangbei women to sit in the one in the back, suddenly saying to her: A Miss! The one in the back still has to wait an hour to open! It's not easy for you to sit. Come, come, come, I'll let you sit here," After saying this, he stood up generously and respectfully offered the seat to the woman, but he himself stood in the place where the Jiangbei women had just stood, that is, in front of the woman. After a while, the bus had already started, and he and she were already talking loudly about "Miss! Mister!" But I don't know if he still remembered that the two Jiangbei women were waiting blankly in the empty car for an hour.

A Meaningful New Year's Card

— Xuefan

Every year at the end of the year, people generally happily look forward to the arrival of the New Year, thinking that the yang is turning to prosperity, and the coming year will have better luck; even people who have a clearer mind and do not believe in fate also recognize that the plan of a year lies in the spring, and the beginning of this spring is indeed worth commemorating. Therefore, over the years, everyone has had the act of congratulating each other on the New Year, and it has been difficult to change the accumulated habits, and they have gradually become a custom.

However, in recent years, New Year's greetings have mostly been replaced by New Year's cards instead of personal door-to-door greetings. However, in this country where the rivers and mountains are broken and the barbarian cavalry are rampant, it would be too ignorant of current affairs to congratulate the New Year in the same way. At least this year's New Year's greetings should contain some impression of the national crisis, and bring some stimulation to the brains that are about to be forgotten. A New Year's card like this is still somewhat meaningful. I have a friend who recently printed a New Year's card, and its wording really wins my heart, so I am eager to transcribe it to share with like-minded people and for observation. The original text is as follows:

"Try to see today's Northeast, whose world is it still? The map has changed color, and the barbarian cavalry are rampant! 400 million people are living drunk and dying dreamily. Where is our ray of light? Young people! Arise, aim our guns forever at our enemies, and jointly save this nation that is about to sink, and jointly awaken this dying national soul. At this time when the yang begins and the earth returns to spring, I hope that you can use new strength to intensify your work, and use new plans to develop your future. Old friend! Time flies, shouldn't you whip it harder? Congratulations on your boundless future!"

Respect "King" Embrace "Queen"<

— Shigong

In these days, even the president is a little tired of playing. The most fashionable, one by one finger counting past, it's the chairman, the member. Whatever "emperor", whatever "king", has already reached the setting sun, it's time to enter the historical museum. Puyi, the chief executive of our Northeast "Manchukuo", knows current affairs. When he gets to the Yellow River, his heart is still not dead. He should be ashamed. The chief executive doesn't want to... Still wants to... Still wants to be lonely and寡德 [phrase meaning virtuous but isolated]. Going against the tide and turning towards me, it can be said that he is abandoning the world.

"Emperor" and "king" are not very fashionable now. The attached "queen" will naturally fall without a fight. But now in the Shanghai market, the atmosphere of restoration is extremely strong. The general big bosses with their chests puffed out and their bellies protruding rack their brains to manufacture something, preventing people from imitating and counterfeiting. So they add a tail to the things they make, calling it "King". In this way, no matter how people imitate and counterfeit, it seems that none can be called a King. For example, a person selling chamber pots calls the chamber pot he sells "Chamber Pot King". A person selling rice buckets calls the rice bucket he sells "Rice Bucket King". Although the motive of this kind of title is only to express that this chamber pot rice bucket is different from other chamber pot rice buckets, it is still suspected that the atmosphere of restoration is too strong and it is somewhat out of step with the trend.

Random Notes from Yue Lu

— Banruo

(1) Winter Lodging

Although she is another corner of society, the appearances within it are no less complicated than a bustling intersection. I remember A-Rong was sentenced to two months in prison for theft. On the day he was released, when he saw the light of day again, everyone knew the joy of regaining freedom. However, A-Rong made an abnormal request. As he pleaded with the warden, tears streamed down his face.

"Thank you, Warden! Please let me stay a few more days. The weather is so freezing, and I can't find work. I don't know what else to do. Kind Warden..."

"Haha! You're treating the prison like a hotel." The warden replied with a comical laugh. He said that to stay in a real hotel, you have to pay for the room. Moreover, in a prison with housing and food, what was he afraid of when facing a lawsuit?

(2) Inscriptions in Prison

If you visit a so-called model prison, you will find inscriptions from master calligraphers, such as commemorative words like "XXX stayed for eight years and four months," or "Heaven will entrust a great task to this person; it must first imprison him." There are even lamentations like "Those who haven't been to prison aren't heroes," and "Those who come here again will become cowards." Thus, one can see that kidnappers, robbers, veteran gunmen, petty crooks, and political prisoners all write and draw like famous people on these walls. It is truly a feast for the eyes. Perhaps the flavor of iron bars is also interesting. There are "Kings" and "Queens." In the highest institutions on whitewashed walls, among the female students of a school, whoever has the best grades, the prettiest face, the slimmest figure, the most fashionable attire, and the most flexible social skills, all on a level playing field, and whose overall average score is the highest, the rest of the students will willingly become slaves under her high heels, and respect her as the "Queen." Originally, if there is a "King," there must be a "Queen." However, since "Great Lord" does not fit the trend, "Queen" is also not in line with the times.

"King" and "Queen" are fashionable now. The old brother among daily newspapers, this newspaper with sixty years of history, can also proudly call itself the "King of Daily Newspapers." This supplement is an appendage of the "King" and can also call itself the "Queen of this Port." However, true gold fears no fire. We certainly don't need to boast like this, using a title that doesn't fit the current trend and has a flavor of restoration. I also think it is superfluous for Puyi to dream of restoring his throne. It is necessary to completely eliminate all the "Kings" and "Queens" of Shanghai. We must not always go backward.

Novel

Writing to a Friend's Wife (Continued from Part 13)

— Qin Shouou

Ah, little brother! The moment she uttered these two sentences, I was so embarrassed that all the muscles in my body tensed up. I wished I could open a window and jump out to escape immediately.

However, beautiful Piglet! Don't panic! I have already decided to risk my life and leave specifically to protect your reputation. At this time, how could I allow her to see through my pretense?

"Haha! Haha!" I used all my strength to grab my heart, preventing it from wavering in the slightest. Then, imitating her madness, I leaned back and forth, laughing heartily.

"Laughter can't cover this up!" She is truly a frightening woman. "That day, Lin Bao-cheng and I saw you and Zhou Dajing's wife at Zhaofeng Park. Weren't you two whispering sweet nothings there?"

She wanted to question me, but she revealed the truth herself first. What relationship did she and Lin Bao-cheng have? What were they doing together at Zhaofeng Park? However, I was also suffering from a guilty conscience, so I couldn't joke with her anymore. I was busy giving you a strong explanation.

"That's not true! You two must have been seeing things!" I tried my best to remain calm, like a pastor.

"Nonsense! Would we not be able to see your ghostly face clearly? As for Dajing's wife, there's still some doubt. But according to Lin Bao-cheng," she actually showed mercy and took three steps back voluntarily. "That person is indeed her. However, you don't need to worry. I will never stir up trouble for others. Besides..."

Her face was completely filled with a kind of contemptuous mockery, which I found unbearable.

"These words are very important. You can't make wild accusations!" I didn't let her continue to be presumptuous and immediately interrupted her. "I can swear to you right now: if I really had such a thing, I will definitely be beheaded or shot within a year! And my descendants will be wiped out, and my flesh and blood will be separated!"

I swore about almost all the facts that were about to come true.

Dear little brother! Swearing is originally a last resort for foolish people. However, in extremely difficult situations, even non-foolish people sometimes have to use it, especially in front of women. Swearing often has a great effect.

"Oh! Why bother! You're still childish!" She really believed that I was wronged because my oath was too earnest and too vicious. "Why swear such a bloody and venomous curse? Actually, I didn't believe there was such a thing. I was just teasing you!"

As soon as she softened, I felt as if I had taken a thousand-pound stone off my back and felt much lighter. It's a pity I didn't know sooner. Now, that little hooligan, Lin Bao-cheng, may still be hiding this secret in his heart. My dearest darling! This is my lifelong regret. Please forgive me especially!

Film Special

Overseas News

Hopes for Anna May Wong

— Ailian

As everyone knows, the only Chinese people with a foothold in Hollywood are Anna May Wong and Yang Aili. She is still studying and cannot be called a star. What can be consoling is that in the artistic world, there is also Wong Chung-Hoh, who has been promoted to the basic photographer of Fox Corporation. Most of Jane Gaynor's major films were shot by Mr. Wong. It is very pitiful that a large country with 500 million people only occupies such a small position in the world's film center.

What's even stranger is that Hollywood's only Chinese female star, Anna May Wong, has been invited to England by Universal Corporation.

England has recently paid great attention to the film industry and plans to completely shift the world's attention to film from Hollywood to the British Isles. This summer, the British government issued an order prohibiting all film stars from leaving the country. At the same time, it used the most generous salaries to attract established American stars and sent special commissioners to reside in Hollywood for a long time. As soon as there was an expired contract or other opportunities, they would immediately seize the opportunity to move the stars to the east coast of the Atlantic. In half a year, they had collected quite a few. Now, our Miss Wong has actually been selected, and we will probably see her in British films soon.

This time, it can be regarded as "honorable behavior" because the position England has given her is much higher than in the United States, allowing her to play at least a supporting role.

Ordinary Chinese people always feel that she is a gold-worshiper with no sense of patriotism, because no matter how many times the Chinese film industry has invited her back to serve her country, she has ignored them. Given the current decline of the Chinese film industry, it certainly cannot offer her the same rich salary as the United States.

She has enjoyed material pleasures but ignored spiritual work. She also acts in films that are unfavorable to China with a fearless spirit, such as "The Red Lantern" more than ten years ago, "The Sea Wolf" seven or eight years ago, and the recent "Shanghai Express." Which of those films did not increase China's shame?

"Let bygones be bygones." There is no need to talk about everything. This time she goes to England, she is the first Chinese actress in Europe. I hope she will no longer be a slave to money and sell her personality. She should show the Europeans the talent and perseverance of the Chinese people, create a new situation, give people a good impression, and win some respect for the country. China will never forget this artistic star, Miss Wong.

Reader Opinions

The Need for Rural Cinemas

— Daosheng

Everyone knows the effect of movies. They are not only works of appreciation, not only entertainment, and not only toys for people to relieve boredom. They have the power to transform society, and they are the best tools to improve society. Indeed, a good film, a meaningful film, has a greater and faster effect than government decrees.

Recently, the government has also realized the importance of film education, considering it a very effective tool for social education, and will make efforts to promote it. Therefore, I feel the need for rural cinemas.

In fact, most of the current cinemas are located in cities. As for the countryside, which has a large number of farmers, there are very few of them. This is of course because the founders of the cinemas only care about monetary gains and do not consider other aspects of income. However, the need for cinemas in the countryside is no less than in the cities. I think that if there were cinemas in the countryside, screening real and meaningful films, the workers and peasants would definitely come happily after work. It is not difficult to achieve the purpose of education through entertainment, enlighten the people, improve habits, and dispel all the shadows in the countryside.

It is best for the government to assist the local administrative authorities in establishing them extensively in the rural areas of each place, providing very low-priced seats for workers and peasants to watch, or even completely free.

The Honor of the Film Industry

— Meicun

The Mayfair Club is the most famous club in California. Many famous socialites and starlets are members. However, in past elections, no actors have been elected as president, and no actresses have been elected as vice president. However, the president elected this year is Frederic March, and the vice president is Norma Shearer. This is an honor for the Hollywood film industry.

Star Biographies

Biography of Mary Pickford

— Wentao

Mary Pickford's films are among the most popular comedies in Hollywood. Especially her style is most easily welcomed by children, because her pure and innocent childlike spirit fully caters to the children's desires. Therefore, more than three million children in the United States enthusiastically support her works. When her films are shown in theaters, the theater owners must sacrifice two-fourths of the seats to these many half-price children! Since she changed her style, the children who welcomed her have become indifferent to her, and at the same time, a large number of children have left.

She is British and grew up in Canada. Her family was very poor. Her father was a tea boy in a theater in New York, so their lives could only be barely sustained. When she was nine years old, because of the lack of financial resources, she joined the theater where her father worked to supplement the family's income as an extra little actress. She earned a dollar a day. Later, her innocent expression, lively posture, and clear singing voice were indeed able to win the praise of the local people. Her reputation became higher and higher day by day. At the age of fifteen, she signed a two-year contract with the theater. Her weekly salary jumped to six hundred yuan. Two years later, when the contract expired, she was hired by United Artists as an actress. From this time on, she began her life on the screen. At the age of eighteen, she married Lowell Sherman, a famous film actor at the time. But soon after, they had disagreements and divorced. After that, she began to work hard under the limelight, and as a result, she became one of the most brilliant movie stars on the screen. At this time, she met Douglas Fairbanks. Their love gradually deepened, and they finally became husband and wife. They were once honored as the queen and king of film, and they were also the most perfect marriage in Hollywood.

Translation of Famous Works

Screen Faces (Continued from Yesterday)

— Dunruo (Translator)

"When shall I come again?" she asked, very puzzled. "We'll let you know when we need you again. There's no certainty," said the one giving her the wages with much amusement. She, quite unaware, went slowly home to wait to be hired again.

In the following months, she was summoned with increasing frequency. In "The Abyss of Voices," her dreary and coldly unsympathetic attitude, walking before a group of women, left a most profound impression upon all who saw the picture; almost every review commented upon this scene, and when this scene was screened, the audience almost stopped their breathing.

Pictures dealing with social problems were very much in vogue that year, and she had become accustomed to performing in crowd scenes; her presence in these scenes always gave them an extra touch of reality.

Trilby Cabasquie was no longer lonely; sometimes when she had not been working for too long she would go to the film company's engagement department. Her hopes gradually grew larger; she hoped to make her career expand so that she could earn more money.

The first money she earned from films she used to pay off the doctor's fees, and for her husband's funeral expenses. She sent her only son, a simpleton who loved playing with matches, to a local home that cared for children with intellectual developmental disabilities. Even though she herself did not earn a great deal, she could, at any rate, breathe a little more freely.

She had lost her job as an extra. Quite luckily, she found a man who rented her spare room. Anton Basch was a widower who made his living selling ice, and he paid twelve marks a month for the room, and half of the gas bill; moreover, he was very affectionate towards her. Wishing to gain Basch's favor, she bought a white cloak. She also made meals for Basch. She made him the sandwiches of sliced meats to take with him when he went out, which made it appear as if she herself ate better food. Gradually the deep hollows and the shadows on her face disappeared. This was now the height of her career. (To be continued)

Letters to the Editor

Editor's esteemed regards: After reading your newspaper's fifteenth issue, I found that the description of Gao William in the "Supplement to Their Leading Men" was not entirely accurate. Mr. Gao himself claims that he has never been to Hollywood and has never played a supporting role with Barrymore. Four years ago, he returned to China from Cuba, where he was engaged in business, and immediately joined the Great Wall Company as a comedian and painter. He has now been hired by the United Company and went to Hong Kong long ago, and is not serving at Lianhua. I am sending this letter to correct the record and hope it will be published for all to see!

Film Reviews

Saturday Revelry? Not Quite?

— Yannan

Hollywood had many new rising stars in 1929. But at the time, some people admitted that the only one who could replace Clara Bow was Nancy Carroll. Her works such as "Honey," "Sweet Kitchen Maid," and "Youth Club" all give us the impression of sweetness and warmth. It has been a long time since we have seen her! Of course, with the big advertisement for "Hot Saturday" revealed at the Grand Theater, everyone will say that this movie is good before seeing it. I'm not here to spoil the fun, but while it's good, it's not as good as it used to be, not as good as we imagined.

The film is still centered on love. She plays a female bank clerk who falls in love with a romantic talent. However, because of the jealousy of another young man, many rumors are fabricated, and she is caught red-handed - not returning home one Saturday night. As a result, she is forced to resign from the bank, and her family does not accept her. At this time, she meets another young scholar. Unexpectedly, she is suspected again because of gossiping. By the time the scholar realizes his mistake, the girl has gone to New York with her old lover, the romantic talent, to get married.

Nancy remains a lovable little deer, being chased by people in the game of love (note: the original name of this film is "Deer Chasing in the Game of Love"). Before the film is finished, there is indeed a feeling of "not knowing who will die at whose hands." She deals with men in a non-committal way, carrying enough of a shy mood of a young girl, but it is also a pity that she has not been able to show her original extremely sweet and warm talent. Although Cary Grant, who plays the romantic talent, is named the protagonist, he performs very little, and his performance can only be said to be good. Randolph Scott, who plays the young scholar, is very good, but there are too many humorous places. Edward Woods is the most beautiful and suits the role the most. However, I think none of these three people are enough to complement our sweet girl.

The whole drama is named "Hot Saturday," and there should be more revelry on Saturday. There is not enough revelry in this film, and the full force is concentrated on "romantic." Therefore, the photography, set design, and lighting are all excellent, presenting the beauty of "full moon and beautiful flowers" and "silence of all sounds" everywhere.

The director is still worth watching. The division of scenes adds a lot of highlights. The sketches of the fragments and the narration of the whole film have their memorable parts. The side shots (dark scenes) are very clever.

The meaning of the film is very superficial, still only talking about the relationship between money and love, and the contradiction between the individual and society. Indeed, it may have the effect of promoting girls to indulge in "revelry." However, if I were to write an advertisement, I would definitely not say it as seriously as Guanglu has published.

Nancy has undoubtedly not made any progress compared to the past. I still say the old saying:

"The movie is very good, very beautiful, and worth watching, but don't expect too much from it beforehand." What do you think, Mr. Bai Gu?
